All information in the news release is furnished but not filed.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:110%">Non-GAAP Financial Information</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the attached news release Accenture discloses the following non-GAAP financial measures:</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Free cash flow (defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions). Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Adjusted financial measures excluding the impact of business optimization costs and gain on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the business optimization costs and the investment gain facilitates an understanding as to the impact of these items and the company&#8217;s performance in comparison to the prior period.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:9pt"><span><br/></span></div><div full-year revenue growth of 8% to 9% in local currency and foreign-exchange impact of negative 4%&#59; GAAP operating margin of 14.2%&#59; adjusted operating margin of 15.4%&#59; GAAP EPS of $10.94 to $11.05&#59; adjusted EPS of $11.52 to $11.63&#59; and free cash flow of $8.1 billion to $8.6 billion --</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; June&#160;22, 2023 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2023, ended May&#160;31, 2023, with revenues of $16.6 billion, an increase of 3% in U.S. dollars and 5% in local currency over the same period last year. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP operating income was $2.36 billion, compared to $2.60 billion for the third quarter last year, and operating margin was 14.2% compared to 16.1% for the third quarter last year. Adjusted operating income was $2.71 billion and adjusted operating margin was 16.3%, an expansion of 20 basis points from the third quarter of fiscal 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted earnings per share were $3.15, compared to $2.79 for the third quarter last year. Adjusted EPS were $3.19, an increase of 14% from the third quarter of fiscal 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the quarter were $17.2 billion, with consulting bookings of $8.9 billion and managed services bookings of $8.3 billion.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:46pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Julie Sweet, chair and CEO, Accenture, said, &#8220;Our third quarter results reflect solid bookings and revenue and very strong adjusted operating margin, earnings per share and free cash flow, which demonstrates the rigor and discipline with which we run our business. The strength of our strategy to be our clients&#8217; transformation partner of choice continues to resonate, with 26 clients with quarterly bookings of $100 million or more&#59; and our business model &#8212; which for decades has been built around the diversity of our markets, industries and services &#8212; along with our more than 730,000 talented people position us well to continue to deliver 360&#176; value for our clients and stakeholders every day.&#8221;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted financial measures presented in this release are non-GAAP financial measures that exclude business optimization costs and a gain related to our investment in Duck Creek Technologies, as further described in this release.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Financial Review</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><br></font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the third quarter of fiscal 2023 were $16.56 billion, compared with $16.16 billion for the third quarter of fiscal 2022, an increase of 3% in U.S. dollars and 5% in local currency. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the quarter reflect a foreign-exchange impact of approximately negative 2.5% compared with the negative 3.5% impact previously assumed. Adjusting for the actual foreign-exchange impact, the company&#8217;s guided range for quarterly revenues was approximately $16.25 billion to $16.85 billion. Accenture&#8217;s third quarter fiscal 2023 revenues were at the midpoint of this adjusted range.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Consulting revenues for the quarter were $8.69 billion, a decrease of 4% in U.S. dollars and 1% in local currency compared with the third quarter of fiscal 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Managed Services revenues were $7.87 billion, an increase of 10% in U.S. dollars and 13% in local currency compared with the third quarter of fiscal 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted EPS for the quarter were $3.15 compared with $2.79 for the third quarter of fiscal 2022. Excluding a $0.42 decrease for business optimization costs and $0.38 increase for a gain on an investment, adjusted EPS were $3.19, an increase of 14% from the third quarter of fiscal 2022. The $0.40 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.12&#160;increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.15&#160;increase from the loss on the disposition of the company&#8217;s business in Russia recorded in fiscal 2022&#59;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.09 increase from a lower effective tax rate&#59;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.04 increase from higher non-operating income&#59; and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01 increase from lower share count&#59; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">      partially offset by</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01&#160;decrease from higher noncontrolling interests.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the quarter was 33.4% compared to 32.9% in the third quarter of fiscal 2022.
